Priority 1 Accessibility


P1 - Manual check

There are some checkpoints that an automatic program like Bobby cannot examine. These 6 item(s) are presented below. You will need to be able to respond affirmatively to these items as well to obtain Bobby Approved status.
  1. Make sure that style sheets transform gracefully.

  2. Ensure that descriptions of dynamic content are updated with changes in content.

  3. If any of the images on this page convey important information beyond what is in each image's alternative text, add descriptive (D) links. (7 instances)
